<p>This is a <b>list of national capitals</b> in alphabetical order, including <a href="/wiki/Territory_(administrative_division)" title="Territory (administrative division)" class="mw-redirect">territories</a> and <a href="/wiki/Dependent_territory" title="Dependent territory">dependencies</a>, non-sovereign states including <a href="/wiki/Associated_state" title="Associated state">associated states</a> and entities whose <a href="/wiki/Sovereignty" title="Sovereignty">sovereignty</a> is <a href="/wiki/Territorial_dispute" title="Territorial dispute">disputed</a>. Sovereign states are shown in bolded text.</p>

<td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/26/Flag_of_the_Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/26/Flag_of_the_Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/26/Flag_of_the_Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="300">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic" title="Sahrawi Arab Democratic Republic">Sahrawi Arab Democratic Republic</a>&nbsp;<sup class="reference" id="ref_cnone"><a href="#endnote_cnone">[c]</a></sup></td>
<td>The Sahrawi Republic, recognised by <a href="/wiki/Legal_status_of_Western_Sahara#States_recognizing_the_SADR" title="Legal status of Western Sahara" class="mw-redirect">82 states</a>, claims the mostly <a href="/wiki/Morocco" title="Morocco">Moroccan</a> controlled <a href="/wiki/Western_Sahara" title="Western Sahara">Western Sahara</a>. Moroccan controlled territory includes El Aaiún, and Morocco claims all <a href="/wiki/Free_Zone_(region)" title="Free Zone (region)">Sahrawi controlled territory</a>. The Sahrawi government resides in exile in <a href="/wiki/Tindouf" title="Tindouf">Tindouf</a>, <a href="/wiki/Algeria" title="Algeria">Algeria</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1"><span>[</span>1<span>]</span></a></sup> See <a href="/wiki/Politics_of_the_Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic" title="Politics of the Sahrawi Arab Democratic Republic">Politics of the Sahrawi Arab Democratic Republic</a>.</td>
</tr>

<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/Jerusalem" title="Jerusalem">Jerusalem</a> <small>(declared, de facto)</small></td>
<td><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Flag_of_Israel.svg/21px-Flag_of_Israel.svg.png" width="21" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Flag_of_Israel.svg/32px-Flag_of_Israel.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Flag_of_Israel.svg/41px-Flag_of_Israel.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="660" data-file-height="480">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a></b></td>
<td><a href="/wiki/Jerusalem_Law" title="Jerusalem Law">Jerusalem Law</a> states that "Jerusalem, complete and united, is the capital of Israel", and the city serves as the seat of the government, home to the president's residence, government offices, supreme court, and parliament. <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council_Resolution_478" title="United Nations Security Council Resolution 478">United Nations Security Council Resolution 478</a> declared the Jerusalem Law "null and void" and called on member states to withdraw their diplomatic missions from Jerusalem. The United Nations and all member states maintain their embassies in other cities such as <a href="/wiki/Tel_Aviv" title="Tel Aviv">Tel Aviv</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ramat_Gan" title="Ramat Gan">Ramat Gan</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Herzliya" title="Herzliya">Herzliya</a>, and do not recognise Jerusalem as the capital.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4"><span>[</span>4<span>]</span></a></sup> Many countries officially adhere to the proposal that Jerusalem have international status, as called for in the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Partition_Plan_for_Palestine" title="United Nations Partition Plan for Palestine">Partition Plan</a> of 1947.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5"><span>[</span>5<span>]</span></a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Palestinian_National_Authority" title="Palestinian National Authority">Palestinian National Authority</a> claims East Jerusalem as the capital of a future Palestinian state. See <a href="/wiki/Positions_on_Jerusalem" title="Positions on Jerusalem">Positions on Jerusalem</a>.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/East_Jerusalem" title="East Jerusalem">East Jerusalem</a> <small>(declared)</small><br>
<a href="/wiki/Ramallah" title="Ramallah">Ramallah</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gaza_City" title="Gaza City">Gaza</a> <small>(de facto)</small></td>
<td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Flag_of_Palestine.svg/23px-Flag_of_Palestine.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Flag_of_Palestine.svg/35px-Flag_of_Palestine.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Flag_of_Palestine.svg/46px-Flag_of_Palestine.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Palestinian_National_Authority" title="Palestinian National Authority">State of Palestine</a></td>
<td>The State of Palestine claims the territories occupied by Israel since the <a href="/wiki/Six-Day_War" title="Six-Day War">Six-Day War</a> in 1967, with <a href="/wiki/East_Jerusalem" title="East Jerusalem">East Jerusalem</a> as its capital. The proclaimed state is currently occupied by Israel and has no effective control over the territories it claims. Administration is based in <a href="/wiki/Ramallah" title="Ramallah">Ramallah</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gaza_City" title="Gaza City">Gaza</a>, rather than Jerusalem. Most members of the United Nations regard East Jerusalem as occupied territory, and the <a href="/wiki/Organisation_of_Islamic_Cooperation" title="Organisation of Islamic Cooperation">Organisation of Islamic Cooperation</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Arab_League" title="Arab League">Arab League</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Non-Aligned_Movement" title="Non-Aligned Movement">Non-Aligned Movement</a> recognise it as the capital of a future Palestinian state.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6"><span>[</span>6<span>]</span></a></sup> See <a href="/wiki/Positions_on_Jerusalem" title="Positions on Jerusalem">Positions on Jerusalem</a>.</td>
</tr>

<td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1e/Flag_of_the_Turkish_Republic_of_Northern_Cyprus.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Turkish_Republic_of_Northern_Cyprus.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1e/Flag_of_the_Turkish_Republic_of_Northern_Cyprus.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Turkish_Republic_of_Northern_Cyprus.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1e/Flag_of_the_Turkish_Republic_of_Northern_Cyprus.svg/45px-Flag_of_the_Turkish_Republic_of_Northern_Cyprus.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1026" data-file-height="684">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Northern_Cyprus" title="Northern Cyprus">Northern Cyprus</a></td>

Northern Cyprus is claimed in whole by the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Cyprus" title="Republic of Cyprus" class="mw-redirect">Republic of Cyprus</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8"><span>[</span>7<span>]</span></a></sup></td>

<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/Pristina" title="Pristina">Pristina</a></td>
<td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/Flag_of_Kosovo.svg/21px-Flag_of_Kosovo.svg.png" width="21" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/Flag_of_Kosovo.svg/32px-Flag_of_Kosovo.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/Flag_of_Kosovo.svg/42px-Flag_of_Kosovo.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="840" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Kosovo" title="Kosovo">Kosovo</a><sup class="reference" id="ref_gnone"><a href="#endnote_gnone">[g]</a></sup></td>
<td>De facto independent state that is recognised by <a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_Kosovo" title="International recognition of Kosovo">108</a> UN member states and by <a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Taiwan</a>. Claimed in whole by the Republic of Serbia as part of its <a href="/wiki/Kosovo" title="Kosovo">Autonomous Province of Kosovo and Metohija</a>. Republic of Kosovo has <i><a href="/wiki/De_facto" title="De facto">de facto</a></i> control over most of the territory, with limited control in <a href="/wiki/North_Kosovo" title="North Kosovo">North Kosovo</a>.</td>

<td><a href="/wiki/Taipei" title="Taipei">Taipei</a></td>
<td><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg/45px-Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Taiwan</a></b></td>
<td>Officially the Republic of China (ROC), it has been competing for recognition with the <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">People's Republic of China</a> (PRC) as the sole Chinese government since 1949. Taiwan controls the island of Taiwan and its associated islands, Quemoy, Matsu, the Pratas, and part of the <a href="/wiki/Spratly_Islands" title="Spratly Islands">Spratly Islands</a><sup id="cite_ref-Spratly_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Spratly-10"><span>[</span>Note 2<span>]</span></a></sup> The territory of Taiwan is claimed in whole by the People's Republic of China.<sup id="cite_ref-TAI2_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TAI2-11"><span>[</span>Note 3<span>]</span></a></sup> The Republic of China participates in the <a href="/wiki/World_Health_Organization" title="World Health Organization">World Health Organization</a> and a number of non-UN international organizations such as the <a href="/wiki/World_Trade_Organization" title="World Trade Organization">World Trade Organization</a>, <a href="/wiki/International_Olympic_Committee" title="International Olympic Committee">International Olympic Committee</a> and others under a variety of pseudonyms, most commonly <a href="/wiki/Chinese_Taipei" title="Chinese Taipei">Chinese Taipei</a>.</td>
</tr>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notes">Notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_national_capitals_in_alphabetical_order&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="reflist" style="list-style-type: decimal;">
<ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-7"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-7"><span class="cite-accessibility-label">Jump up </span>^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="/wiki/Cusco" title="Cusco">Cusco</a> city was declared by the art. 49 of the Peruvian Constitution as "Historical Capital" (in Spanish <i>Capital Histórica</i>), a statement merely symbolic.</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-Spratly-10"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-Spratly_10-0"><span class="cite-accessibility-label">Jump up </span>^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The sovereignty over the <a href="/wiki/Spratly_Islands" title="Spratly Islands">Spratly Islands</a> is disputed by the PRC, the ROC, <a href="/wiki/Vietnam" title="Vietnam">Vietnam</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a> (part), <a href="/wiki/Malaysia" title="Malaysia">Malaysia</a> (part), and <a href="/wiki/Brunei" title="Brunei">Brunei</a> (part). Except Brunei, each of these countries occupies part of the islands (see <a href="/wiki/List_of_territorial_disputes" title="List of territorial disputes">List of territorial disputes</a>).</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-TAI2-11"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-TAI2_11-0"><span class="cite-accessibility-label">Jump up </span>^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">In 1949, the Republic of China government led by the <a href="/wiki/Kuomintang" title="Kuomintang">Kuomintang</a> (KMT) lost the <a href="/wiki/Chinese_Civil_War" title="Chinese Civil War">Chinese Civil War</a> to the <a href="/wiki/Communist_Party_of_China" title="Communist Party of China">Communist Party of China</a> (CPC) and set up a provisional capital in Taipei. The CPC established the People's Republic. As such, the <a href="/wiki/Political_status_of_Taiwan" title="Political status of Taiwan">political status</a> of the ROC and the <a href="/wiki/Legal_status_of_Taiwan" title="Legal status of Taiwan" class="mw-redirect">legal status of Taiwan</a> (alongside the <a href="/wiki/Free_Area_of_the_Republic_of_China" title="Free Area of the Republic of China" class="mw-redirect">territories</a> currently under ROC jurisdiction) are in dispute. In 1971, the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> gave the <a href="/wiki/China_and_the_United_Nations" title="China and the United Nations">China seat</a> to the PRC instead of the ROC: most states recognize the PRC to be the <a href="/wiki/One-China_policy" title="One-China policy">sole legitimate representative of all China</a>, and the UN classifies Taiwan as "<a href="/wiki/Taiwan_Province,_People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="Taiwan Province, People's Republic of China">Taiwan, Province of China</a>". The ROC has <i>de facto</i> relations with most sovereign states. A significant political movement within Taiwan advocates <a href="/wiki/Taiwan_independence" title="Taiwan independence" class="mw-redirect">Taiwan independence</a>.</span></li>
</ol>
</div>
